    THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
END, [dto.Tag].[Name], [dto.Tag].[Type]
FROM [ProductTags] AS [x.Products.ProductTags]
INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [dto.Tag] ON [x.Products.ProductTags].[TagId] = [dto.Tag].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [t0].[ParentId], [t0].[Id], [x.Products0].[Id] AS [Id0]
    FROM [Products] AS [x.Products0]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [x1].[ParentId], [x1].[Id]
        FROM [ProductCategories] AS [x1]
    ) AS [t0] ON [x.Products0].[CategoryId] = [t0].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [x.Products.ProductTags].[ProductId] = [t1].[Id0]
ORDER BY [t1].[ParentId], [t1].[Id], [t1].[Id0]" (0723d8ff)
